class]”. This attribute’s default value is _false_ . This customization
eases preserving simple type substituting precisely as described in
link:jaxb.htm#50536464_90601[See Type Substitution of a Simple Type
Definition]”.
* [#50536467_pgfId-1097205]## _localScoping_ attribute can have the
value of either _nested_ or _toplevel_ . This attribute describes the
JAXB binding of nested XML schema component to either a _nested_
schema-derived JAXB class or a _toplevel_ schema-derived JAXB class. To
avoid naming collisions between nested components, the default value for
this attribute is _nested_ . A developer can customize _localScoping_ to
_toplevel_ w hen schema components nest too deeply or an application
would prefer to not work with nested classes.

[#50536467_pgfId-1077595]##The semantics of the above customization
values, if not specified above, are specified when they are actually
used in the binding declarations.

[#50536467_pgfId-1099883]##For inline annotation, a _<globalBindings>_
is valid only in the annotation element of the _<schema>_ element. There
must only be a single instance of a _<globalBindings>_ declaration in
the annotation element of the _<schema>_ element.

==== [#50536467_pgfId-1099886]##[#50536467_37846]##Customized Name Mapping

[#50536467_pgfId-1077600]##A customization value can be used to specify
a name for a Java object (e.g. class name, package name etc.). In this
case, a customization value is referred to as a customization name.

[#50536467_pgfId-1077601]##A customization name is always a legal Java
identifier (this is formally specified in each binding declaration where
the name is specified). Since customization deals with customization of
a Java representation to which an XML schema element is bound, requiring
a customization name to be a legal Java identifier rather than an XML
name is considered more meaningful.

[#50536467_pgfId-1077602]##A customization name may or may not conform
to the recommended Java language naming conventions. [JLS - Java
Language Specification, Second Edition, Section 6.8, “Naming
Conventions”]. The customization value enableJavaNamingConventions
determines if a customization name is mapped to a Java identifier that
follows Java language naming conventions or not.

[#50536467_pgfId-1077603]##If enableJavaNamingConventions is defined and
the value is _"true"_ or _"1",_ then the customization name (except for
constant name) specified in the section from where this section is
referenced must be mapped to Java identifier which follows the Java
language naming conventions as specified in
link:jaxb.htm#50536475_85614[See Conforming Java Identifier Algorithm]”;
otherwise the customized name must be used as is.

==== [#50536467_pgfId-1077608]##[#50536467_78312]##Underscore Handling

[#50536467_pgfId-1097037]##The _[jaxb:globalBindings]_ attribute
customization _underscoreBinding_ allows for the preservation of
underscore(s) occurring in an XML name when deriving a a Java identifier
from it.

[#50536467_pgfId-1097041]##The default value for _@underscoreBinding_ is
_"asWordSeparator"_ and categorizes underscore, ‘_’, as a punctuation
mark in the XML name to Java identifier algorithm specified in Appendix
link:jaxb.htm#50536475_21536[See The Name to Identifier Mapping
Algorithm]. The resulting algorithm transforms one or more consecutive
underscores in an XML name to camel case separated words in the derived
Java class and method names. Examples of this mapping are in
link:jaxb.htm#50536475_11629[See XML Names and derived Java Class,
Method, and Constant Names].

[#50536467_pgfId-1096955]##When @ _underscoreBinding_ is
_"asCharInWord",_ underscore (‘_’) is considered a special letter within
a word. The result is that all underscore characters from the original
XML name are preserved in the derived Java identifier. Example of this
mapping are in link:jaxb.htm#50536475_78570[See XML Names and derived
Java Class, Method, and Constant Names when <jaxb:globalBindings
underscoreHandling=”asCharInWord”>].

==== [#50536467_pgfId-1094825]##[#50536467_47895]##generateElementClass and generateValueClass

[#50536467_pgfId-1094831]##The following code examples illustrate
default binding to value class and customization to bind to
interface/implementation classes.

======= [#50536467_pgfId-1094832]##Default Binding to a value class.

[#50536467_pgfId-1094833]##Schema fragment:

[#50536467_pgfId-1095048]##<xs:complexType name=”USAddress”> +
<xs:attribute name=”City” type=”xs:string”/>

[#50536467_pgfId-1095052]##</xs:complexType>

[#50536467_pgfId-1095373]## Default Value Class:

[#50536467_pgfId-1095374]##public class USAddress \{ +
public USAddress() \{... } +
public String getCity() \{....} +
public void setCity(String value) \{...} +
... +
}

[#50536467_pgfId-1095393]##Customization _<jaxb:globalBinding
generateValueClass=”false”>_ generates following interface instead of
default value class:

======= [#50536467_pgfId-1095412]##Customized binding to an interface.

[#50536467_pgfId-1096240]##public interface USAddress \{ +
String getCity(); +
void setCity(String value); +
}

======= [#50536467_pgfId-1094842]##Generation of an Element Class

[#50536467_pgfId-1095082]##Schema fragment:

[#50536467_pgfId-1095083]##<xs:element name=”Address”
type=”USAddress”/> +
 +
// Default Java binding of global element to element instance factory +
public ObjectFactory \{ +
JAXBElement<USAddress> createAddress(USAddress value); +
}

[#50536467_pgfId-1094843]## _<jaxb:globalBinding
generateElementClass=”true”/>_ results in generation of following
Element class:

[#50536467_pgfId-1096250]## +
public class Address extends JAXBElement<USAddress> \{ +
}

==== [#50536467_pgfId-1096595]##[#50536467_71010]##@typesafeEnumMemberName

[#50536467_pgfId-1096608]##.If there is a collision among the generated
constant fields _name_ or if it is not possible to generate a legal Java
identifier for one or more of the generated constant field names, then
the binding is determined based on the value of @
_typesafeEnumMemberName_ of element _[jaxb:globalBindings]_ .

* [#50536467_pgfId-1096609]## _skipGeneration +
_ An enum type is not generated. This is the default behavior if
_typesafeEnumMemberName_ has not been specified. A binding compiler may
report a warning on why the simple type definition was not bound to an
enum type.
* [#50536467_pgfId-1096632]## _generateName +
_ The constant fields _name_ is “ _VALUE__ _<N>_ _"_ where _<N>_ is 1
for the first enumeration value and increments by 1 to represent each
value within the XML enumeration.
* [#50536467_pgfId-1096631]## _generateError +
_ An error must be reported.

==== [#50536467_pgfId-1097246]##<serializable> Declaration

[#50536467_pgfId-1096076]##When the serializable customization is
specified, all schema-derived classes implement _java.io.Serializable_ .
Each class is generated with a _serialVersionUID_ field set to the value
specified by _@uid_ .

[#50536467_pgfId-1096132]##private static final long serialVersionUID =
_<value of @uid>_ ;

[#50536467_pgfId-1096171]##The JAXB user is required to identify when
schema-derived classes do not follow
_http://java.sun.com/j2se/1.4.2/docs/guide/serialization/spec/version.html#wp4602[Java
serialization class evolution rules]_ and change the generated
_serialVersionUID_ field by changing the [serializable] element’s
attribute _@uid_ value.

==== [#50536467_pgfId-1099940]##@generateElementProperty

[#50536467_pgfId-1099950]##Some schemas use both minOccurs="0" on
element as well as nillable="true", causing the generation of
JAXBElement. This customization lets you control this behavior. This
attribute may take two values:

* [#50536467_pgfId-1100002]## _true: +
_ Always generate properties to use JAXBElement, unless overriden by
_<jaxb:property generateElementProperty=”false”/>_ on individual
property.
* [#50536467_pgfId-1100083]## _false: +
_ When generating properties from _<element nillable=”true”
minOccurs=”0”/>_ , generate a property not to use JAXBElement, as if the
element declaration were just _<element nillable=”true” />_ , unless
overriden by _<jaxb:property generateElementProperty=”true”/>_ on
individual property. It is an error to specify this customization, when
the property is required to be JAXBElement (such as when a property
contains multiple elements with different names but of the same type.)

== [#50536467_pgfId-1077612]##[#50536467_32461]## _<schemaBindings>_ Declaration

[#50536467_pgfId-1077613]##The customization values in
_<schemaBindings>_ binding declaration have schema scope. This binding
declaration is therefore useful for customizing at a schema level.

==== [#50536467_pgfId-1077614]##Usage

[#50536467_pgfId-1077615]##<schemaBindings [ map="boolean" ] >

{empty}[#50536467_pgfId-1077616]## [ <package> package </package> ]

[#50536467_pgfId-1077617]## [ <nameXmlTransform> ... </nameXmlTransform>
]*

[#50536467_pgfId-1077618]##</schemaBindings>

[#50536467_pgfId-1077619]##

{empty}[#50536467_pgfId-1077620]##<package [ name = "packageName" ]

{empty}[#50536467_pgfId-1077621]## [ <javadoc> ... </javadoc> ]

[#50536467_pgfId-1077622]##</package>

[#50536467_pgfId-1077623]## 

[#50536467_pgfId-1077624]##<nameXmlTransform>

{empty}[#50536467_pgfId-1077625]## [ <typeName [ suffix="suffix" ]

{empty}[#50536467_pgfId-1077626]## [ prefix="prefix" ] /> ]

{empty}[#50536467_pgfId-1077627]## [ <elementName [ suffix="suffix" ]

{empty}[#50536467_pgfId-1077628]## [ prefix="prefix" ] /> ]

{empty}[#50536467_pgfId-1077629]## [ <modelGroupName [ suffix="suffix" ]

{empty}[#50536467_pgfId-1077630]## [ prefix="prefix" ] /> ]

{empty}[#50536467_pgfId-1077631]## [ <anonymousTypeName [
suffix="suffix" ]

{empty}[#50536467_pgfId-1077632]## [ prefix="prefix" ] /> ]

[#50536467_pgfId-1077633]##</nameXmlTransform>

[#50536467_pgfId-1093994]##For readability, the _<nameXmlTransform>_ and
_<package>_ elements are shown separately. However, they are local
elements within the _<schemaBindings>_ element.

[#50536467_pgfId-1077635]##The following customizations are defined in
the schema scope:

* [#50536467_pgfId-1100236]## _map_ if specified, prevents the classes
from being generated from this schema. When the value is “0” or “false”,
then no class/interface/enum will be generated from this package. map
defaults to true.

[#50536467_pgfId-1100235]##The semantics of the customization value, if
not specified above, are specified when they are actually used in the
binding declarations.

[#50536467_pgfId-1077636]##For inline annotation, a _<schemaBindings>_
is valid only in the annotation element of the _<schema>_ element. There
must only be a single instance of a _<schemaBindings>_ declaration in
the annotation element of the _<schema>_ element.

[#50536467_pgfId-1077637]##If one source schema includes (via the
include mechanism specified by XSD PART 1) a second source schema, then
the _<schemaBindings>_ declaration must be declared in the first
including source schema. It should be noted that there is no such
restriction on _<schemaBindings>_ declarations when one source schema
imports another schema since the scope of _<schemaBindings>_ binding
declaration is schema scope.

===== [#50536467_pgfId-1077639]##package __ [#50536467_75884]##

[#50536467_pgfId-1077640]##Usage

* [#50536467_pgfId-1077641]## _name_ if specified, defines the
customization value _packageName_ . _packageName_ must be a valid Java
package name.
* [#50536467_pgfId-1077642]##< _javadoc>_ if specified, customizes the
package level Javadoc. < _javadoc>_ must be specified as described in
link:jaxb.htm#50536467_64915[See <javadoc> Declaration].” The Javadoc
must be generated as specified in link:jaxb.htm#50536467_50461[See
Javadoc Customization].” The Javadoc section customized is the _package
section._
* [#50536467_pgfId-1077649]##

[#50536467_pgfId-1077650]##The semantics of the _packageName_ is
specified in the context where it is used. If neither _packageName_ nor
the < _javadoc>_ element is specified, then the binding declaration has
no effect.

====== [#50536467_pgfId-1077651]##Example: Customizing Package Name

[#50536467_pgfId-1077652]##<jaxb:schemaBindings>

[#50536467_pgfId-1077653]## <jaxb:package name = "org.example.po" />

[#50536467_pgfId-1077654]##</jaxb:schemaBindings>

[#50536467_pgfId-1077655]##specifies “ _org.example.po_ ” as the package
to be associated with the schema.

===== [#50536467_pgfId-1077656]## _nameXmlTransform_

[#50536467_pgfId-1077657]##The use case for this declaration is the UDDI
Version 2.0 schema. The UDDI Version 2.0 schema contains many
declarations of the following nature:

[#50536467_pgfId-1077658]##<xs:element name="bindingTemplate"
type="uddi:bindingTemplate"/>

[#50536467_pgfId-1077659]##The above declaration results in a name
collision since both the element and type names are the same - although
in different XML Schema symbol spaces. Normally, collisions are supposed
to be resolved using customization. However, since there are many
collisions for the UDDI V2.0 schema, this is not a convenient solution.
Hence the binding declaration _nameXmlTransform_ is being provided to
automate name collision resolution.

[#50536467_pgfId-1077660]##The _nameXmlTransform_ allows a _suffix_ and
a _prefix_ to be specified on a per symbol space basis. The following
symbol spaces are supported:

* [#50536467_pgfId-1077661]## _<typeName>_ for the symbol space “type
definitions”
* [#50536467_pgfId-1077662]## _<elementName>_ for the symbol space
“element definitions”
* [#50536467_pgfId-1077663]## _<modelGroupName>_ for the symbol space
“model group definitions.”
* [#50536467_pgfId-1077664]## _<anonymousTypeName>_ for customizing Java
value class to which an anonymous type is bound.link:#pgfId-1077667[26]

[#50536467_pgfId-1077668]##If _suffix_ is specified, it must be appended
to all the default XML names in the symbol space. The _prefix_ if
specified, must be prepended to the default XML name. Furthermore, this
XML name transformation must be done after the XML name to Java
Identifier algorithm is applied to map the XML name to a Java
identifier. The XML name transformation must not be performed on
customization names.

[#50536467_pgfId-1077669]##By using a different _prefix_ and/or _suffix_
for each symbol space, identical names in different symbol spaces can be
transformed into non-colliding XML names.

[#50536467_pgfId-1077670]## _anonymousTypeName_

[#50536467_pgfId-1093985]##The _<anonymousTypeName>_ declaration can be
used to customize the suffix and prefix for the Java value class. If
_prefix_ is specified, then it must be prepended to the Java value class
name for the anonymous type. If suffix is specified, it must be
appended.

== [#50536467_pgfId-1093987]## _<class>_ [#50536467_41898]## Declaration

[#50536467_pgfId-1077676]##This binding declaration can be used to
customize the binding of a schema component to an element class, value
class or interface/implementation class. The customizations can be used
to specify:

* [#50536467_pgfId-1077677]##a name for the derived Java class.
* [#50536467_pgfId-1099599]##an alternative implementation of
interface/implementation binding.

[#50536467_pgfId-1077679]##Specification of an alternate implementation
for an interface allows implementations generated by a tool (e.g. based
on UML) to be used in place of the default implementation generated by a
JAXB provider.

[#50536467_pgfId-1077680]##The implementation class may have a
dependency upon the runtime of the binding framework. Since a runtime
was not specified for JAXB 1.0 interface/implementation binding, the
implementation class may not be portable across JAXB provider
implementations. Hence one JAXB provider implementation is not required
to support the implementation class from another JAXB provider.

==== [#50536467_pgfId-1077681]##Usage

{empty}[#50536467_pgfId-1077682]##<class [ name = " _className_ " ]

{empty}[#50536467_pgfId-1077683]## [ implClass = " _implClass_ " ]> +
[ ref = " _className_ " ]

{empty}[#50536467_pgfId-1094958]## [ <javadoc> _..._ </javadoc> ]

[#50536467_pgfId-1077685]##</class>

* [#50536467_pgfId-1077686]## _className_ is the name of the derived
value class, if specified. It must be a legal Java class name and must
not contain a package prefix. The package prefix is inherited from the
current value of package _._
* [#50536467_pgfId-1077687]## _implClass_ if specified, is the name of
the implementation class for _className_ and must include the complete
package name. Note that this customization only impacts the return value
for _className_ ’s factory method. This customization is ignored when
_new_ is used to create instances of a schema-derived Value class.
* [#50536467_pgfId-1100251]## _ref_ if specified, is the name of the
value class that is provided outside the schema compiler. This
customization causes a schema compiler to refer to this external class,
as opposed to generate a definition. It must include the complete
package name. This attribute is mutually exclusive with the _className_
attribute and the _implClass_ attribute.
* [#50536467_pgfId-1077688]## _<javadoc>_ element, if specified
customizes the Javadoc for the derived value class. _<javadoc>_ must be
specified as described in link:jaxb.htm#50536467_64915[See <javadoc>
Declaration].”

==== [#50536467_pgfId-1077693]##[#50536467_61445]##Customization Overrides

[#50536467_pgfId-1077694]##When binding a schema element’s Java
representation to a value class or a Java Element class, the following
customization values override the defaults specified in Chapter 5. It is
specified in a common section here and referenced from
link:jaxb.htm#50536467_34303[See Customizable Schema Elements].”

* [#50536467_pgfId-1077698]##name: The name is _className_ if specified.
* [#50536467_pgfId-1077699]##package name: The name of the package is
_packageName_ inherited from a scope that covers this schema element. +
 +
NOTE: The _packageName_ is only set in the <package> declaration. The
scope of _packageName_ is schema scope and is thus inherited by all
schema elements within the schema.
* [#50536467_pgfId-1077700]##javadoc: The Javadoc must be generated as
specified in section link:jaxb.htm#50536467_50461[See Javadoc
Customization].” The Javadoc section customized is the _class/interface
section._

==== [#50536467_pgfId-1077705]##[#50536467_34303]##Customizable Schema Elements

===== [#50536467_pgfId-1077706]##Complex Type Definition

[#50536467_pgfId-1077707]##When _<class>_ customization specified in the
annotation element of the complex type definition, the complex type
definition must be bound to a Java value class as specified in
link:jaxb.htm#50536464_33754[See Java value class]” applying the
customization overrides as specified in link:jaxb.htm#50536467_61445[See
Customization Overrides].”

====== [#50536467_pgfId-1077714]##Example: Class Customization: Complex Type Definition To Java value class

[#50536467_pgfId-1077715]##XML Schema fragment:

[#50536467_pgfId-1077716]##<xs:complexType name="USAddress"> +
<xs:annotation> <xs:appinfo> +
<jaxb:class name="MyAddress" /> +
</xs:appinfo></xs:annotation> +
<xs:sequence>...</xs:sequence> +
<xs:attribute name="country" type="xs:string"/> +
</xs:complexType>

[#50536467_pgfId-1077722]##Customized code:

[#50536467_pgfId-1077723]##// public class USAddress \{ // Default Code

[#50536467_pgfId-1077724]##public class MyAddress \{ // Customized Code

[#50536467_pgfId-1077725]## public String getCountry()\{...}

[#50536467_pgfId-1077726]## public void setCountry(String value)\{...}

[#50536467_pgfId-1077727]## ...

[#50536467_pgfId-1077728]##}

===== [#50536467_pgfId-1097134]##Simple Type Definition

[#50536467_pgfId-1097135]##When _<class>_ customization specified in the
annotation element of a simple type definition, the simple type
definition must be bound to a Java value class as specified in
link:jaxb.htm#50536464_16362[See Bind to a JAXB mapped class]” applying
the customization overrides as specified in
link:jaxb.htm#50536467_61445[See Customization Overrides].”

====== [#50536467_pgfId-1097142]##Example: Class Customization: Simple Type Definition To Java value class

[#50536467_pgfId-1097143]##XML Schema fragment:

[#50536467_pgfId-1097144]##<xs:simpleType name="SKU"> +
<xs:annotation> <xs:appinfo> +
<jaxb:class/> +
</xs:appinfo></xs:annotation> +
<xs:restriction base=”xs:int”/> +
</xs:simpleType>

[#50536467_pgfId-1097145]##Customized code:

[#50536467_pgfId-1097147]##public class SKU \{ +
@XmlValue +
public int getValue()\{...} +
public void setValue(int value)\{...} +
... +
}

===== [#50536467_pgfId-1097132]##[#50536467_23951]##Model Group Definition

[#50536467_pgfId-1095432]##It is invalid to place a _<jaxb:class>_
customization on a model group.

===== [#50536467_pgfId-1077760]##[#50536467_33012]##Model Group

[#50536467_pgfId-1095429]##It is invalid to place a _<jaxb:class>_
customization on an unnamed model group.

===== [#50536467_pgfId-1077768]##Global Element Declaration

[#50536467_pgfId-1077769]##A < _class_ > declaration is allowed in the
annotation element of the global element declaration. However, the
_implClass_ attribute is not allowed. The global element declaration
must be bound as specified in link:jaxb.htm#50536464_60943[See Bind to
Element Class]” applying the customization overrides specified in
link:jaxb.htm#50536467_61445[See Customization Overrides].”

====== [#50536467_pgfId-1077776]##Example: Class Customization: Global Element to Class

[#50536467_pgfId-1077777]##XML Schema Fragment:

[#50536467_pgfId-1077778]##<xs:complexType name="AComplexType">

[#50536467_pgfId-1077779]## <xs:sequence>

[#50536467_pgfId-1077780]## <xs:element name="A" type="xs:int"/>

[#50536467_pgfId-1077781]## <xs:element name="B" type="xs:string"/>

[#50536467_pgfId-1077782]## </xs:sequence>

[#50536467_pgfId-1093239]##</xs:complexType>

[#50536467_pgfId-1077783]##<xs:element name="AnElement"
type="AComplexType">

[#50536467_pgfId-1077784]## <xs:annotation><xs:appinfo>

[#50536467_pgfId-1077785]## <jaxb:class name="MyElement"/>

[#50536467_pgfId-1077786]## </xs:appinfo></xs:annotation>

[#50536467_pgfId-1077787]##</xs:element>

[#50536467_pgfId-1077788]##Customized code:

[#50536467_pgfId-1077797]##// following class is generated because of
customization

[#50536467_pgfId-1093905]##public class AComplexType \{ +
void setA(int value) \{...}

[#50536467_pgfId-1093906]## int getA()\{...}

[#50536467_pgfId-1093907]## void setB(String value)\{...}

[#50536467_pgfId-1093908]## String getB()\{...}

[#50536467_pgfId-1077798]##}

[#50536467_pgfId-1099780]##public class MyElement extends
JAXBElement<AComplexType> \{...}

[#50536467_pgfId-1077799]##public class ObjectFactory \{

[#50536467_pgfId-1093926]## // Default code

[#50536467_pgfId-1099796]## // JAXBElement<AnElement>
createAnElement(AnElement)\{...} +
 +
// Customized code

[#50536467_pgfId-1099797]## MyElement createMyElement(AnElement)\{...} +
... other factory methods ...

[#50536467_pgfId-1077804]##}

===== [#50536467_pgfId-1077805]##Local Element

[#50536467_pgfId-1077806]##A local element is a schema element that
occurs within a complex type definition. A local element is one of:

* [#50536467_pgfId-1077807]##local element reference (using the “ref”
attribute) to a global element declaration.
* [#50536467_pgfId-1077808]##local element declaration (“ref” attribute
is not used).

[#50536467_pgfId-1077809]##A _<class>_ declaration is allowed in the
annotation element of a local element. link:jaxb.htm#50536467_30958[See
Annotation Restrictions]” contains more information regarding the
annotation element for a local element reference. However, the
_implClass_ attribute is not allowed.

[#50536467_pgfId-1077813]##A _<class>_ customization on local element
reference must result in an invalid customization as specified in
link:jaxb.htm#50536467_20413[See Invalid Customizations]” since a local
element reference is never bound to a Java Element class.

[#50536467_pgfId-1077817]##A _<class>_ customization on local element
declaration applies only when a local element declaration is bound to a
Java Element class. Otherwise it must result in an invalid customization
as specified in link:jaxb.htm#50536467_20413[See Invalid
Customizations].” If applicable, a local element must be bound as
specified in link:jaxb.htm#50536464_94772[See Bind to JAXBElement<T>
Instance]” applying the customization overrides as specified in
link:jaxb.htm#50536467_61445[See Customization Overrides].”

====== [#50536467_pgfId-1077827]##Example: Class Customization: Local Element Declaration To Java Element

[#50536467_pgfId-1077831]##The following example is from
link:jaxb.htm#50536464_67519[See Examples].”

[#50536467_pgfId-1077832]##XML Schema fragment:

[#50536467_pgfId-1077833]##<xs:complexType name="Base"> +
<xs:choice maxOccurs="unbounded"> +
<xs:element name="A" type="xs:string"> +
<xs:annotation><xs:appinfo> +
<jaxb:class name="Bar"/> +
< _/xs:appinfo></xs:annotation> +
_ </xs:element> +
<xs:element name="B" type="xs:string"/> +
<xs:element name="C" type="xs:int"/> +
</xs:choice> +
</xs:complexType>

[#50536467_pgfId-1077842]##Customized code:

[#50536467_pgfId-1077843]##import javax.xml.bind.JAXBElement; +
public class ObjectFactory \{ +
// element instance factories only +
// JAXBElement<String> createBaseA(String value); //default code +
JAXBElement<String> createBaseBar(String value); //Customized +
JAXBElement<String> createBaseB(String value); +
JAXBElement<Integer> createBaseC(Integer value); +
} +
public class Base \{ +
static public class Bar extends JAXBElement<String> \{...}// Customized
code +
/** +
* A general content list that can contain element +
* instances of JAXBElement<String> or JAXBElement<Integer>. +
*/ +
List<Object> getBarOrBOrC()\{...} +
}

== [#50536467_pgfId-1077859]##[#50536467_28399]## _<property>_ Declaration

[#50536467_pgfId-1077860]##This binding declaration allows the
customization of a binding of an XML schema element to its Java
representation as a property. This section identifies all XML schema
elements that can be bound to a Java property and how to customize that
binding.

[#50536467_pgfId-1077861]##The scope of customization value can either
be definition scope or component scope depending upon which XML schema
element the < _property>_ binding declaration is specified.

==== [#50536467_pgfId-1077863]##[#50536467_55656]##Usage

[#50536467_pgfId-1077864]##<property [ name = "propertyName" ] +
[ collectionType = " _propertyCollectionType_ " ] +
[ fixedAttributeAsConstantProperty = "true" | "false" | "1" | "0" ] +
[ generateIsSetMethod = "true" | "false" | "1" | "0" ] +
[ enableFailFastCheck="true" | "false" | "1" | "0" ] +
[ generateElementProperty= “true” | “false” | “1” | “0” ] +
[ attachmentRef = “resolve” | “doNotResolve” | “default” ] +
[ <baseType name=”fully qualified Java class”> ... </baseType> ] +
[ <javadoc> ... </javadoc> ] +
</property> +
 +
<baseType name=”fully qualified Java class”> +
<javaType> ... </javaType> +
</baseType>

[#50536467_pgfId-1077876]##For readability, the _<baseType>_ element is
shown separately. However, it can be used only as a local element within
the _<property>_ element.

[#50536467_pgfId-1082545]##The use of this declaration is subject to the
constraints specified in link:jaxb.htm#50536467_72724[See Usage
Constraints].”

[#50536467_pgfId-1077877]##The customization values defined are:

* [#50536467_pgfId-1077878]## _name_ if specified , defines the
customization value _propertyName;_ it must be a legal Java identifier.
* [#50536467_pgfId-1077880]## _collectionType_ if specified, defines the
customization value _propertyCollectionType_ which is the collection
type for the property. _propertyCollectionType_ if specified, must be
either “ _indexed"_ or any fully qualified class name that implements
_java.util.List._
* [#50536467_pgfId-1077881]## _fixedAttributeAsConstantProperty_ if
specified , defines the customization value
_fixedAttributeAsConstantProperty_ . The value must be one of _"true",
false", "1" or"0"._
* [#50536467_pgfId-1077882]## _generateIsSetMethod_ if specified,
defines the customization value of _generateIsSetMethod._ The value must
be one of _"true", false", "1" or"0"._
* [#50536467_pgfId-1100124]## _enableFailFastCheck_ if specified,
defines the customization value _enableFailFastCheck._ The value must be
one of _"true", false", "1" or"0"._
* [#50536467_pgfId-1100200]## _@generateElementProperty_ if specified,
controls the generation of JAXBElement property. The value must be one
of "true", "false", "1", or "0". The default is absence of the value. It
is an error for this attribute to be present if this customization is
attached to local or global attribute declarations. This customization
affects the binding as follows. It is an error to specify this
customization, when the property is required to be _JAXBElement_ (such
as when a property contains multiple elements with different names but
of the same type.)
* [#50536467_pgfId-1100169]## _true_ : Always generate properties to use
_JAXBElement_ .
* [#50536467_pgfId-1100178]## _false_ : When generating properties from
_<element nillable="true" minOccurs="0" />_ , generate a property not to
use JAXBElement, as if the element declaration were just _<element
nillable="true"/>_ .
* [#50536467_pgfId-1100171]## _@attachmentRef_ has a default value of
“default”. This mode defers to default processing as specified in
link:jaxb.htm#50536486_42506[See Binding WS-I Attachment Profile
ref:swaRef]”. +
 +
When _@attachmentRef_ value is _resolve_ and the property’s base type is
or derives from _xsd:anyURI_ , the schema-derived JAXB property has a
base type of _javax.activation.DataHandler_ and the property is
annotated with _@XmlAttachmentRef_ . +
 +
Disabling autoresolving an element/attribute of type _ref:swaRef_ : +
When _@attachmentRef_ value is _doNotResolve_ and the property’s base
type derives from standard schema type _ref:swaRef,_ the schema-derived
JAXB property has the base type _String_ , derived from _xsd:anyURI,_
and _@XmlAttachmentRef_ is not generated for the property.
* [#50536467_pgfId-1096303]## _<javadoc>_ element, if specified
customizes the Javadoc for the property’s getter method. _<javadoc>_
must be specified as described in link:jaxb.htm#50536467_64915[See
<javadoc> Declaration].”

==== [#50536467_pgfId-1077888]## _baseType_ [#50536467_98204]##

[#50536467_pgfId-1077889]##The _<baseType>_ element is intended to allow
the customization of a base type for a JAXB property. This element can
only be a child of <jaxb:property> element.

[#50536467_pgfId-1099390]##<baseType name=”fully qualified Java
class”> +
<javaType> ... </javaType> +
</baseType>

[#50536467_pgfId-1099443]## 

[#50536467_pgfId-1099444]##The _@name_ attribute enables either the
specialization or generalization of the default base type binding for a
JAXB property. Child element _<javaType>_ is used to convert the default
base type to a Java class. These two mutual exclusive usages of the
<baseType> customization are described below.

===== [#50536467_pgfId-1097301]##[#50536467_89562]##Conversion using Child element <javaType>

[#50536467_pgfId-1097326]##Optional child element < _javaType>_ , if
specified, defines the customization value _javaType_ and must be
specified as defined in link:jaxb.htm#50536467_72052[See <javaType>
Declaration].” The customization value defined has component scope. This
customization converts the default base type’s value for a simple type
definition to the Java class specified by <javaType> name.

[#50536467_pgfId-1097510]##The schema-derived JAXB property is annotated
with _@XmlJavaTypeAdapter_ specified in Section 8.
_@XmlJavaTypeAdapter.value()_ is set to a generated
classlink:#pgfId-1097563[27] that extends
_javax.xml.bind.annotation.adapter.XmlAdapter_ . The generated class’
_unmarshal_ method must call the <javaType> customization’s parse
method, which is specified in link:jaxb.htm#50536467_72052[See
<javaType> Declaration]. The generated class’ _marshal_ method must call
the <javaType> customization’s print method.

===== [#50536467_pgfId-1079085]##[#50536467_30760]##Generalize/Specialize baseType with attribute @name

[#50536467_pgfId-1097313]##The _name_ attribute for _<baseType>_ enables
more precise control over the actual base type for a JAXB property. This
customization enables specifying an alternative base type than the
property’s default base type. The alternative base type must still be in
the same class inheritance hierarchy as the default base type. The
alternative base type must be either a super interface/class or subclass
of the default Java base type for the property. The customization
enables one to specialize or generalize the properties binding.

[#50536467_pgfId-1097486]##The _name_ attribute value must be a fully
qualified Java class name. When the default base type is a primitive
type, consider the default Java base type to be the Java wrapper class
of that primitive type.

[#50536467_pgfId-1097357]##Generalizing the basetype using this
customization enables simple type substitution for a JAXB property
representing with too restrictive of a default base type. To enable all
possible valid type substitutions, the _name_ attribute should be
_java.lang.Object_ . However, if for example, it is known that all type
substitutions will share a more specific Java super interface/class than
_java.lang.Object_ , that Java class name can be used achieve a stronger
typed binding. With this customization, the JAXB annotation generated
for the property’s _@XmlElement.type()_ or _@XmlAttribute.type()_ is
still the default Java datatype for the element/attribute’s
schema-defined type.

[#50536467_pgfId-1097398]##The schema-derived customized JAXB property
is annotated, either explicitly or by default mapping annotations, with
the mapping annotation _@XmlElement_ , specified in Section 8.10.1. The
_@XmlElement_ annotation element type is derived in terms of the
abstract model properties for a element type definition summarized in
link:jaxb.htm#50536458_10343[See Element Declaration Schema Component]
as follows:

======= [#50536467_pgfId-1097419]##Annotate JAXB property with @XmlElement element-value pairs

[width="100%",cols="50%,50%",options="header",]
|===
|[#50536467_pgfId-1097404]##@XmlElement element
|[#50536467_pgfId-1097406]##@XmlElement value
|[#50536467_pgfId-1097416]##type |[#50536467_pgfId-1097418]##the java
type binding of the element declaration’s _\{type definition}_
|===

[#50536467_pgfId-1097420]##Note that the Java class for
_@XmlElement.type()_ can differ from the recommended JAXB property’s
base type to enable type substitution of java.lang.Object. This binding
enables unmarshalling of the Element’s simple content when it is not
qualified with an _xsi:type_ as the element’s schema-declared type.
_@XmlElement.type()_ acts as the default _xsi:type_ for a JAXB property
where the property’s base type was generalized to allow for type
substitution of an element declaration with a simple type definition.

[#50536467_pgfId-1099375]##Specializing the basetype using this
customization generates stronger typing than default JAXB binding. For
example, an XML element or attribute of _xs:IDREF_ binds to
_java.lang.Object_ by default as specified in
link:jaxb.htm#50536464_52889[See Binding an IDREF component to a Java
property]”. If the schema only intends the reference to be to an element
that binds to a specific type, the baseType @name schema customization
can be used to specialize the binding.

======= [#50536467_pgfId-1099397]##[#50536467_67079]##Specialize binding of an IDREF via customization

[#50536467_pgfId-1099398]##Given XML Schema fragment:

[#50536467_pgfId-1099399]##<xs:complexType name="Book"> +
<xs:sequence> +
_<xs:element name="author" type="xs:IDREF"/> +
_ _<xs:annotation><xs:appinfo> +
<jaxb:property> +
<jaxb:baseType name=”AuthorBio.class”/> +
</jaxb:property> +
</xs:appinfo></xs:annotation> +
_ <!-- ... --> +
</xs:sequence> +
</xs:complexType> +
<xs:complexType name="AuthorBio"> +
<xs:sequence><!-- ... --> </xs:sequence> +
_<xs:attribute name="name" type="xs:ID"/> +
_ </xs:complexType>

[#50536467_pgfId-1099400]##Schema-derived Java value class:

[#50536467_pgfId-1099401]##public class Book \{ +
@XmlIDREF +
AuthorBio getAuthor() \{...} +
void setAuthor(AuthorBio referencedObj)\{...} +
} +
public class AuthorBio\{ +
@XmlID +
String getName()\{...} +
void setName(String value)\{...} +
}

===== [#50536467_pgfId-1082546]##[#50536467_72724]##Usage Constraints

[#50536467_pgfId-1082547]##The usage constraints on _<property>_ are
specified below. Any constraint violation must result in an invalid
customization as specified in link:jaxb.htm#50536467_20413[See Invalid
Customizations].” The usage constraints are:

. [#50536467_pgfId-1082568]##The _<baseType>_ is only allowed with the
following XML schema elements from the link:jaxb.htm#50536467_68077[See
Customizable Schema Elements]”:
. [#50536467_pgfId-1082572]##Local Element,
link:jaxb.htm#50536467_61018[See Local Element].”
. [#50536467_pgfId-1082579]##Local Attribute,
link:jaxb.htm#50536467_28343[See Local Attribute].”
. [#50536467_pgfId-1084854]##ComplexType with simpleContent,
link:jaxb.htm#50536467_24088[See ComplexType].”
. [#50536467_pgfId-1097336]##<baseType> can either have a name attribute
or a <javaType>, they both can not exist at the same time.
. [#50536467_pgfId-1082564]##The _fixedAttributeAsConstantProperty_ is
only allowed with a local attribute, link:jaxb.htm#50536467_28343[See
Local Attribute]" , that is fixed.
. [#50536467_pgfId-1082730]##If a _<property>_ declaration is associated
with the _<complexType>_ , then a _<property>_ customization cannot be
specified on the following schema elements that are scoped to
_<complexType>_ :
. [#50536467_pgfId-1083335]##Local Element
. [#50536467_pgfId-1083336]##Model group
. [#50536467_pgfId-1083341]##Model Group Reference

[#50536467_pgfId-1082757]##The reason is that a _<property>_ declaration
associated with a complex type binds the content model of the complex
type to a general content property. If a _<property>_ declaration is
associated with a schema element listed above, it would create a
conflicting customization.

* [#50536467_pgfId-1083744]##

====== [#50536467_pgfId-1077892]##Example: Property Customization: simple type customization

[#50536467_pgfId-1077893]##<xs:complexType name="internationalPrice"> +
.... +
<xs:attribute name="currency" type="xs:string"> +
<xs:annotation> <xs:appinfo> +
<jaxb:property> +
<jaxb:baseType> +
<jaxb:javaType name="java.math.BigDecimal" +
parseMethod="javax.xml.bind.DatatypeConverter.parseInteger" +
printMethod="javax.xml.bind.DatatypeConverter.printInteger"/> +
</jaxb:baseType> +
</jaxb:property> +
</xs:appinfo></xs:annotation> +
</xs:attribute> +
</xs:complexType>

[#50536467_pgfId-1077899]##The code generated is:

[#50536467_pgfId-1077900]##public class InternationalPrice \{

[#50536467_pgfId-1077902]## // String getCurrency(); default

[#50536467_pgfId-1077903]## java.math.BigDecimal getCurrency()\{...} //
customized

[#50536467_pgfId-1077904]## public void setCurrency(java.math.BigDecimal
val)\{...} // customized

[#50536467_pgfId-1077909]##}

==== [#50536467_pgfId-1077912]##[#50536467_81943]##Customization Overrides

[#50536467_pgfId-1077913]##When binding a schema element’s Java
representation to a property, the following customization values
override the defaults specified in Chapter 6. It is specified in a
common section here and referenced from link:jaxb.htm#50536467_68077[See
Customizable Schema Elements].”

* [#50536467_pgfId-1077917]##name: If propertyName is defined, then it
is the name obtained by mapping the name as specified in
link:jaxb.htm#50536467_37846[See Customized Name Mapping].”
* [#50536467_pgfId-1077921]##base type: The basetype is
_propertyBaseType_ if defined. The propertyBaseType is defined by a XML
schema element in link:jaxb.htm#50536467_68077[See Customizable Schema
Elements].”
* [#50536467_pgfId-1077922]##collection type: The collection type is
_propertyCollectionType_ if specified; otherwise it is the
_propertyCollectionType_ inherited from a scope that covers this schema
element.
* [#50536467_pgfId-1077923]##javadoc: The Javadoc must be generated as
specified in section link:jaxb.htm#50536467_50461[See Javadoc
Customization].” The Javadoc section customized is the _method section._
* [#50536467_pgfId-1077927]##If _propertyBaseType_ is a Java primitive
type and _propertyCollectionType_ is a class that implements
java.util.List, then the primitive type must be mapped to its wrapper
class.

[#50536467_pgfId-1077928]##The following does not apply if local
attribute is being bound to a constant property as specified in
link:jaxb.htm#50536467_28343[See Local Attribute]”:

* [#50536467_pgfId-1077932]##If generateIsSetMethod is “true” or “1”,
then additional methods as specified in link:jaxb.htm#50536473_50692[See
isSet Property Modifier]” must be generated.
* [#50536467_pgfId-1077936]##If enableFailFastCheck is “true” or “1”
then the type constraint checking when setting a property is enforced by
the JAXB implementation. Support for this feature is optional for a JAXB
implementation in this version of the specification.

==== [#50536467_pgfId-1077938]##[#50536467_68077]##Customizable Schema Elements

===== [#50536467_pgfId-1077939]##Global Attribute Declaration

[#50536467_pgfId-1077940]##A < _property_ > declaration is allowed in
the annotation element of the global attribute declaration.

[#50536467_pgfId-1077941]##The binding declaration does not bind the
global attribute declaration to a property. Instead it defines
customization values that have definition scope. The definition scope
covers all local attributes (link:jaxb.htm#50536467_28343[See Local
Attribute]”) that can reference this global attribute declaration. This
is useful since it allows the customization to be done once when a
global attribute is defined instead of at each local attribute that
references the global attribute declaration.

===== [#50536467_pgfId-1077946]##[#50536467_28343]##Local Attribute

[#50536467_pgfId-1077947]##A local attribute is an attribute that occurs
within an attribute group definition, model group definition or a
complex type. A local attribute can either be a

* [#50536467_pgfId-1077948]##local attribute reference (using the “ref”
attribute) to a global attribute declaration.
* [#50536467_pgfId-1077949]##local attribute declaration (“ref”
attribute is not used).

[#50536467_pgfId-1082657]##A < _property_ > declaration is allowed in
the annotation element of a local
attribute.link:jaxb.htm#50536467_30958[See Annotation Restrictions]”
contains more information regarding the annotation element for a local
attribute reference. The customization values must be defined as
specified in link:jaxb.htm#50536467_55656[See Usage]” and have component
scope.

[#50536467_pgfId-1082664]##If _javaType_ is defined, then the
_propertyBaseType_ is defined to be Java datatype specified in the
_"name"_ attribute of the _javaType_ .

* [#50536467_pgfId-1082665]##If _fixedAttributeAsConstantProperty_ is “
_true"_ or “ _1"_ and the local attribute is a fixed, the local
attribute must be bound to a Java Constant property as specified in
link:jaxb.htm#50536464_66138[See Bind to a Java Constant property]”
applying customization overrides as specified in
link:jaxb.htm#50536467_81943[See Customization Overrides].” The
generateIsSetMethod, choiceContentProperty and enableFailFastCheck must
be considered to have been set to false.
* [#50536467_pgfId-1077966]##Otherwise, it is bound to a Java property
as specified in link:jaxb.htm#50536464_77839[See Attribute use]”
applying customization overrides as specified in
link:jaxb.htm#50536467_81943[See Customization Overrides].”

====== [#50536467_pgfId-1077971]##Example: Customizing Java Constant Property

===== [#50536467_pgfId-1078018]##[#50536467_56148]##Global Element Declaration

[#50536467_pgfId-1078019]##A _<property>_ declaration is allowed in the
annotation element of a global element declaration. However, the usage
is constrained as follows:

[#50536467_pgfId-1078024]##The binding declaration does not bind the
global element declaration to a property. Instead it defines
customization values that have definition scope. The definition scope
covers all local elements (link:jaxb.htm#50536467_61018[See Local
Element]”) that can reference this global element declaration. This is
useful since it allows the customization to be done once when a global
element is defined instead of at each local element that references the
global element declaration.

===== [#50536467_pgfId-1078029]##[#50536467_61018]##Local Element

[#50536467_pgfId-1078030]##A local element is a schema element that
occurs within a complex type definition. A local element is one of:

* [#50536467_pgfId-1078031]##local element reference (using the “ref”
attribute) to a global element declaration.
* [#50536467_pgfId-1078032]##local element declaration (“ref” attribute
is not used).

[#50536467_pgfId-1078033]##A <property> declaration is allowed in the
annotation element of a local element. link:jaxb.htm#50536467_30958[See
Annotation Restrictions]” contains more information regarding the
annotation element for a local element reference.

[#50536467_pgfId-1078046]##The customization values must be defined as
specified in link:jaxb.htm#50536467_55656[See Usage]” and have component
scope.

[#50536467_pgfId-1078049]##If _javaType_ is defined, then the
_propertyBaseType_ is defined to be Java datatype specified in the
_"name"_ attribute of the _javaType_ .

[#50536467_pgfId-1083320]##The local element must be bound as specified
in link:jaxb.htm#50536464_77835[See Content Model Default Binding]”
applying customization overrides as specified in
link:jaxb.htm#50536467_81943[See Customization Overrides].”

[#50536467_pgfId-1078056]##See example in
link:jaxb.htm#50536467_93152[See Example 3: Property Customization:
Model Group To Content Property Set]” in section
link:jaxb.htm#50536467_90787[See Model Group].”

===== [#50536467_pgfId-1078115]##Wildcard

[#50536467_pgfId-1078116]##A _<property>_ declaration is allowed in the
annotation element of the wildcard schema component. The customization
values must be defined as specified in link:jaxb.htm#50536467_55656[See
Usage]” and have component scope.

[#50536467_pgfId-1078120]##The wildcard schema component must be bound
to a property as specified in link:jaxb.htm#50536464_63210[See Bind
wildcard schema component]” applying customization overrides as
specified in link:jaxb.htm#50536467_81943[See Customization Overrides].”

[#50536467_pgfId-1078127]##Example: The following schema example is from
UDDI V2.0

[#50536467_pgfId-1078128]##<xs:complexType name="businessEntityExt">

[#50536467_pgfId-1078129]## <xs:sequence>

[#50536467_pgfId-1078131]## <xs:any namespace="##other"

[#50536467_pgfId-1078132]## processContents="strict"

[#50536467_pgfId-1078133]## minOccurs="1" maxOccurs="unbounded">

[#50536467_pgfId-1078134]## <xs:annotation><xs:appinfo>

[#50536467_pgfId-1078135]## <jaxb:property name="Extension"/>

[#50536467_pgfId-1078136]## </xs:appinfo></xs:annotation>

[#50536467_pgfId-1078137]## </xs:any>

[#50536467_pgfId-1078138]## ....

[#50536467_pgfId-1078139]## </xs:sequence>

[#50536467_pgfId-1078140]##</xs:complexType>

[#50536467_pgfId-1078141]##Customized derived code:

[#50536467_pgfId-1078142]##public class BusinessEntityExt \{

[#50536467_pgfId-1078143]## ...

[#50536467_pgfId-1078144]## // List getAny(); // Default Code

[#50536467_pgfId-1078145]## List getExtension()\{...} // Customized Code

[#50536467_pgfId-1078146]##}

===== [#50536467_pgfId-1078148]##[#50536467_90787]##Model Group

[#50536467_pgfId-1078149]##A _<property>_ binding declaration is allowed
in the annotation element of the compositor (i.e. _<choice>_ ,
_<sequence>_ or _<all>_ ). The customization values must be defined as
specified in link:jaxb.htm#50536467_55656[See Usage]” and have component
scope.

[#50536467_pgfId-1095937]##The customized binding of a model group is
determined by the following:

* [#50536467_pgfId-1095946]## _choiceContentProperty_ attribute in
_<globalBindings>_ .
* [#50536467_pgfId-1083066]##If propertyBaseType is defined and a
_<property>_ declaration is also present, then the customization
overrides specified in link:jaxb.htm#50536467_81943[See Customization
Overrides]” must be applied by the model group’s parent schema element
to the property used to aggregate the Java value class.
* [#50536467_pgfId-1080869]##If propertySet is defined, then the model
group’s parent schema element must aggregate the property set as
specified in link:jaxb.htm#50536464_52752[See Aggregation of Property
Set].”

====== [#50536467_pgfId-1078168]##Example1: Property Customization: Model Group To ChoiceContent Property

[#50536467_pgfId-1078169]##XML Schema fragment

[#50536467_pgfId-1078170]##<xs:annotation><xs:appinfo> +
<jaxb:globalBindings choiceContentProperty="true"/> +
</xs:appinfo></xs:annotation>

[#50536467_pgfId-1083103]##<xs:complexType name=”AType”> +
<xs:choice>

[#50536467_pgfId-1078174]## <xs:element name="foo" type="xs:int"/>

[#50536467_pgfId-1078175]## <xs:element name="bar" type="xs:string"/>

[#50536467_pgfId-1078176]## </xs:choice> +
</xs:complexType>

[#50536467_pgfId-1078177]##Customized derived code:

[#50536467_pgfId-1078178]##class ObjectFactory \{ +
JAXBElement<Integer> createAtypeFoo(Integer value); +
JAXBElement<String> createAtypeBar(String value);

[#50536467_pgfId-1093939]##} +
public class AType \{ +
void setFooOrBar(Object o)\{...} //customized code +
Object getFooOrBar()\{...} //customized code +
}

[#50536467_pgfId-1078181]##The _choiceContentProperty_ is required to
bind the choice model group to a choice content property.

/** +
* A general content list that can contain +

*/ +

====== [#50536467_pgfId-1078210]##[#50536467_93152]##Example 3: Property Customization: Model Group To Content Property Set

[#50536467_pgfId-1093750]##<xs:complexType name="USAddress"/> +

</xs:appinfo></xs:annotation> +
